I was on fire, why would I wake him up and ask you to open the door! He hesitated again, and later saw that I was angry and opened the door for me. Late, I don't want to stay now, the room fee for the next day is non-refundable)

I thought that all the people who came to stay in the five-star hotel were on business trips. The professional quality of the hotel service needs to be improved.
Let's see how Ctrip's customer service handles it, listen to me patiently, think from the customer's point of view with empathy, and fight for me. I want to tell the Kempinski Hotel that I don't want you to free the room, and it's not an embarrassment. I want your service and attitude.
This stay has zero experience! Five-star hotels should pay more attention to the quality of service. Hope your hotel needs to be improved. Not worth the price and star rating!
